Question #339 (ID: 44915)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What does the term 'quantum' refer to?

Options:


Correct Answer: The smallest discrete quantity of any physical property.

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: A "quantum" is defined as the smallest discrete (indivisible) amount of a physical quantity that can be exchanged or measured.  
Step 2: For example, in electromagnetic radiation the energy of a photon is given by [math]E = h
u[/math], where [math]h[/math] is Planck's constant and [math]
u[/math] the frequency; this shows energy is delivered in discrete quanta (photons).  
Step 3: Therefore the correct meaning is "the smallest discrete quantity of any physical property." Other plausible choices like "a wave" or "a continuous amount" are incorrect because quantum theory specifically refers to discrete (not continuous) packets of physical quantities.

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #340 (ID: 44916)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Which scientist is known for formulating the theory of quantum mechanics?

Options:
a. Isaac Newton
b. Niels Bohr
c. Albert Einstein
d. Max Planck


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Identify who introduced the idea of energy quanta — in 1900 Max Planck proposed that electromagnetic energy is emitted in discrete quanta and gave the relation [math]E = h
u[/math], where [math]h[/math] is Planck's constant and [math]
u[/math] is frequency.
Step 2: Because this quantization idea solved the blackbody radiation problem and founded quantum theory, Max Planck is credited with formulating the theory of quantum mechanics.
Brief note on other options: Isaac Newton developed classical mechanics, Niels Bohr later built a quantum-based atomic model, and Albert Einstein explained the photoelectric effect using quanta — but none of them originally formulated the quantum theory.

Explanation:

Question #341 (ID: 44917)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Quantum physics can explain phenomena at the macroscopic level.

Options:
a. True
b. False


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
সমাধান:
ধাপ ১: কোয়ান্টাম পদার্থবিজ্ঞান মাইক্রোস্কোপিক কণা (অণু, ইলেকট্রন, ফোটন ইত্যাদি)–এর আচরণ ব্যাখ্যা করে এবং তাদের উপর নির্ভর করে থাকা নিয়ম (যেমন তăț্বিক অবস্থাসমূহ, তরঙ্গ-সংকোচন ইত্যাদি) দেয়।  
ধাপ ২: ম্যাক্রোস্কোপিক স্তরের অধিকাংশ দৈনন্দিন দৃশ্য এবং ক্লাসিক্যাল গুণাগুণ (যেমন গ্যাসের চাপ, তাপমাত্রা, বলবেগের গতিবিজ্ঞান) সাধারণত ক্লাসিক্যাল পদার্থবিজ্ঞানে বা স্ট্যাটিস্টিক্যাল মেকানিক্সে ব্যাখ্যা করা হয়; কোয়ান্টাম প্রভাব সাধারণভাবে টুকরো টুকরো অনুবর্তীভাবে সম্মিলিত হয়ে এমার্জেন্ট বৈশিষ্ট্য তৈরি করে।  
ধাপ ৩: বিশেষ পরিস্থিতিতে (উদাহরণ: সুপারকন্ডাক্টিভিটি, সুপারফ্লুইডিটি, বোজ-আইনস্টাইন কনডেন্সেট) কোয়ান্টাম প্রভাব ম্যাক্রোস্কোপিকভাবে প্রকাশ পায়, কিন্তু এই বিশেষ খণ্ডগুলিকে সাধারণ ম্যাক্রোস্কোপিক সকল ঘটনার সমতুল্য বলা যায় না। 

অতএব মূল বিবৃতিটি সার্বজনীনভাবে ভুল — সঠিক উত্তর: b (False)।  
কেন a ভুল: বিবৃতিটি অতিরঞ্জিত করে কোয়ান্টাম তত্ত্বকে সব ম্যাক্রোস্কোপিক ঘটনা ব্যাখ্যা করতে সক্ষম বলছে, যা সাধারণভাবে সঠিক নয়; বেশিরভাগ ম্যাক্রোস্কোপিক আচরণ ক্লাসিক্যাল বা এমার্জেন্ট তত্ত্ব দিয়ে বোঝানো হয়।

Explanation:

Question #342 (ID: 44918)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The dual nature of light is described as __________.

Options:
a. Wave and Particle
b. Solid and Liquid
c. Mass and Energy
d. Static and Dynamic


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
সমাধান:
ধাপে ধাপে ব্যাখ্যা:
1) আলো দুটি ভিন্ন বৈশিষ্ট্য প্রদর্শন করে — তরঙ্গগত বৈশিষ্ট্যে আলোর ইন্টারফেরেন্স ও ডিফ্র্যাকশন দেখা যায় (যেমন ইয়ং-এর দ্বৈত ফাঁক পরীক্ষায়), এবং কণাগত বৈশিষ্ট্যে ফোটোইলেকট্রিক প্রভাব দেখা যায়।  
2) ফোটোইলেকট্রিক প্রভাব বোঝায় আলোর কণা (ফোটন) হিসেবে আচরণ করে; ফোটনের শক্তি সম্পর্কিত সূত্রটি হলো [math]E = hf[/math] (এখানে [math]h[/math] প্লাঙ্ক ধ্রুবক, [math]f[/math] কম্পান)। তাই আলোর দ্বৈত প্রকৃতি হলো তরঙ্গ ও কণার সমন্বয়।  
3) অতএব সঠিক উত্তর হল a: Wave and Particle। অন্য অপশনগুলো ভুল কারণ "Solid and Liquid" এবং "Static and Dynamic" আলোর প্রকৃতির সাথে সম্পর্কিত নয়, আর "Mass and Energy" বিভ্রান্তিকর — আলো শক্তি বহন করে কিন্তু বিশ্রামে বস্তুগত ভর ধার্য হয় না।

Explanation:

Question #343 (ID: 44919)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What is one of the key experiments in quantum physics?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
Solution: The double-slit experiment is a key experiment because it directly demonstrates wave–particle duality: individual photons or electrons produce an interference pattern when not measured, yet behave like particles when which-path information is obtained. Method: particles pass through two closely spaced slits and the screen intensity shows interference fringes whose spacing is given by [math]y=\frac{\lambda D}{d}[/math] (where [math]\lambda[/math] is wavelength, [math]D[/math] is distance to the screen, and [math]d[/math] is slit separation), matching wave predictions. Other famous experiments (photoelectric effect shows quantization of light, Stern–Gerlach shows spin quantization) are important, but the double-slit uniquely illustrates both wave and particle aspects, so the correct answer is the double-slit experiment.

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #344 (ID: 44920)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What does quantum tunneling allow particles to do?

Options:
a. Travel faster than light
b. Pass through barriers
c. Gain mass
d. Change charge


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Solution:
1. Quantum tunneling is the phenomenon where a particle with energy less than a potential barrier can still be be found on the other side because its wavefunction penetrates and decays inside the barrier (classically forbidden region).  
2. For a simple rectangular barrier the transmission (tunneling) probability falls off roughly like [math]T \approx e^{-2\kappa a}[/math] with [math]\kappa = \sqrt{2m(U-E)}/\hbar[/math], showing nonzero chance to pass through for [math]E<U[/math].  
3. Therefore the correct choice is b: pass through barriers.  
4. The other options are incorrect: a (travel faster than light) would violate relativity, c (gain mass) and d (change charge) contradict conservation laws and are not consequences of tunneling.

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #345 (ID: 44921)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
All particles are identical in quantum physics.

Options:
a. True
b. False


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
সমাধান:
1. প্রশ্নের অর্থ বুঝা: বলা হচ্ছে "সমস্ত কণাই কোয়ান্টাম পদার্থবিজ্ঞানে অভিন্ন" — এটি যদি বোঝায় যে সব কণার অভ্যন্তরীণ বৈশিষ্ট্য (ভর, চার্জ, স্পিন) একই, তবে এটি সঠিক নয়।
2. কারণ: বিভিন্ন কণার বিভিন্ন ভর, চার্জ ও স্পিন থাকে (যেমন ইলেকট্রন ও প্রোটন ভিন্ন), তাই সব কণা অভিন্ন নয়। একই প্রজাতির কণাগুলোকে কোয়ান্টামে "অসনাক্তযোগ্য" বা identical বলা হয় যার ফলে তরঙ্গফাংশা সমীকরণকে সাম্যকৃত/অ্যান্টিসাম্যকৃত করা হয় (বোসনদের জন্য সিমেট্রিক, ফার্মিয়নদের জন্য অ্যান্টিসিমেট্রিক)।
3. সুতরাং মূল বিবৃতিটি ভুল; সঠিক উত্তর: b (False)। a ভুল কারণ এটি বিভিন্ন প্রজাতির কণার বৈশিষ্ট্যগত পার্থক্য অস্বীকার করে।

Explanation:

Question #346 (ID: 44922)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In quantum mechanics, the mathematical function that describes the quantum state of a system is called a __________.

Options:
a. Wave Function
b. Probability Density
c. Quantum Field
d. State Vector


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
The mathematical function that describes the quantum state in nonrelativistic quantum mechanics is the wave function, usually written as [math]\psi(x,t)[/math]. The physical content (probability density) is given by the Born rule [math]|\psi(x,t)|^2[/math], so the wave function itself is the primary mathematical object (option a). Option b (Probability Density) is the square modulus of the wave function, option c (Quantum Field) refers to fields in quantum field theory rather than the usual single-particle wave function, and option d (State Vector) is an abstract, equivalent representation ([math]|\psi\rangle[/math]) but the question asks for the function specifically. Correct answer: a.

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #347 (ID: 44923)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What is the significance of the Planck constant?

Options:


Correct Answer: It relates energy to frequency.

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: The Planck constant h expresses the proportionality between a photon's energy and its frequency by the relation [math]E = h
u[/math].  
Step 2: Numerically, [math]h \approx 6.626\times 10^{-34}\ \mathrm{J\cdot s}[/math], so a photon of frequency [math]
u[/math] has energy given by the formula above.  
Step 3: This means energy is quantized in units proportional to frequency, which underlies phenomena like blackbody radiation and the photoelectric effect.  
Brief note on alternatives: it does not directly give momentum–wavelength relation (that is de Broglie: [math]p = h/ \lambda[/math]) nor is it a constant of speed or charge; its primary significance is the energy–frequency relation.

Explanation:

Solution:

Critical thinking involves evaluating __________.

Options:
a. Emotional responses
b. Arguments and evidence
c. Social interactions
d. Personal beliefs


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Define critical thinking — it is the deliberate process of analyzing, assessing, and judging the validity and strength of reasons, arguments, and supporting information.  
Step 2: Compare options — "arguments and evidence" directly match that definition, while "emotional responses" and "personal beliefs" are subjective inputs that critical thinking seeks to examine rather than accept, and "social interactions" are contexts where thinking occurs but not the central focus.  
Step 3: Conclude — the best choice is b because critical thinking specifically involves evaluating arguments and evidence to reach justified conclusions.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To improve critical thinking, one should practice __________.

Options:
a. Listening actively
b. Ignoring feedback
c. Relying on intuition
d. Accepting all opinions


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Critical thinking requires gathering information, evaluating arguments, and recognizing assumptions; these skills improve when you understand others' viewpoints.  
Step 2: Practicing active listening helps you notice evidence, ask clarifying questions, and test assumptions, so it directly develops critical-thinking abilities — therefore option (a) is correct.  
Step 3: Options (b) ignoring feedback prevents learning, (c) relying solely on intuition can introduce bias, and (d) accepting all opinions without evaluation stops you from judging merit — none of these foster critical thinking.

Question #352 (ID: 44928)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A key component of critical thinking is the ability to __________.

Options:
a. Synthesize information
b. Avoid contradictions
c. Accept authority
d. Follow trends


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Define the core of critical thinking — it involves analyzing, evaluating, and combining information to form reasoned conclusions.  
Step 2: Compare options: (a) "Synthesize information" directly matches the idea of combining and evaluating evidence; (b) "Avoid contradictions" is desirable but only one aspect of logical consistency; (c) "Accept authority" contradicts critical thinking’s emphasis on independent evaluation; (d) "Follow trends" is passive and not part of critical analysis.  
Conclusion: therefore the correct answer is (a) Synthesize information.

Explanation:

Question #353 (ID: 44929)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Critical thinkers often ask __________ questions.

Options:
a. Closed
b. Leading
c. Open-ended
d. Rhetorical


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Critical thinking requires exploration, evidence, reasoning and multiple possible answers rather than a single yes/no response.  
Step 2: Open-ended questions prompt explanation, analysis and justification, so they best support critical thinking.  
Step 3: The other options are less suitable: closed questions (a) elicit yes/no answers, leading questions (b) bias responses, and rhetorical questions (d) do not expect an answer.  
Therefore the correct answer is c: Open-ended.

Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In critical thinking, it is essential to recognize __________.

Options:
a. Biases and assumptions
b. Facts and figures
c. Emotional reactions
d. Social norms


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Critical thinking means examining arguments and the reasons behind claims; a key part of that is finding hidden biases and unstated assumptions that can skew judgment.  
Step 2: Once biases and assumptions are recognized, you can evaluate evidence more objectively and avoid being misled.  
Therefore the correct answer is a: Biases and assumptions. Options b (facts and figures), c (emotional reactions) and d (social norms) are relevant factors to consider, but the essential foundational skill in critical thinking is identifying biases and assumptions.

Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Effective critical thinking can lead to better __________.

Options:
a. Decision-making
b. Socializing
c. Persuasion
d. Memorization


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Identify the core idea — effective critical thinking involves analyzing information, evaluating evidence, and comparing alternatives.  
Step 2: Match to the options — these skills directly improve one's ability to choose among options and predict consequences, so they most directly lead to better decision-making.  
Step 3: Eliminate other choices — socializing is an interpersonal skill, persuasion is about influencing others (which may use critical thinking but is not its primary outcome), and memorization is rote recall rather than analytic evaluation.  
Therefore the correct answer is a: Decision-making.

Options:
a. Strengths
b. Weaknesses
c. Popularity
d. Trends


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Solution: Step 1: Critical thinking means analyzing claims, reasons, evidence, and assumptions to judge whether an argument is valid and well-supported. Step 2: In that analysis one looks for logical errors, unsupported premises, biases and fallacies—these are the weaknesses in an argument. Therefore the correct answer is (b) Weaknesses. Options (a) Strengths is partly true but the key purpose here is to detect flaws; (c) Popularity and (d) Trends are not relevant to logical evaluation.

Step 3: Eliminate the others — silence, isolation, and conformity (b, c, d) discourage exchange of ideas or critical evaluation, so they do not enhance critical thinking. Therefore the correct answer is (a) Debate.

Question #362 (ID: 44938)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In critical thinking, it is important to differentiate between __________.

Options:
a. Fact and opinion
b. Emotion and logic
c. Truth and lies
d. Knowledge and ignorance


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: In critical thinking we aim to evaluate claims objectively, so first distinguish between a fact (an objectively verifiable statement) and an opinion (a subjective belief or preference).  
Step 2: This distinction matters because facts can be checked with evidence, while opinions require different handling (e.g., identifying underlying assumptions or values).  
Step 3: Other options are related but less central: emotion vs logic (helps evaluate reasoning but emotions can coexist with both facts and opinions), truth vs lies (concerns veracity but doesn’t handle subjective claims), knowledge vs ignorance (broader epistemic states).  
Therefore the best answer is (a) fact and opinion.

Explanation:

The other options are incorrect because limiting critical thinking to only science, only arts, or only business ignores its universal role as a transferable skill useful in all domains.

The process of critical thinking includes __________.

Options:
a. Reflective thinking
b. Blind acceptance
c. Emotional decision-making
d. Avoiding analysis


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Define the core of critical thinking — it is a deliberate, reflective, and analytical process of evaluating information and forming reasoned judgments.  
Step 2: Compare each option to that definition:
- a Reflective thinking — matches the definition and is a central component of critical thinking.  
- b Blind acceptance — contradicts critical thinking because it requires no evaluation.  
- c Emotional decision-making — may influence decisions but is not the systematic, evidence-based process that defines critical thinking.  
- d Avoiding analysis — directly opposes the analytical nature of critical thinking.  
Conclusion: The correct answer is a (Reflective thinking) because it aligns with the purposeful, evaluative nature of critical thinking.

c. Luck
d. Conformity


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:

Step 1: Regularly engage in exercises that require analysis, evaluation, and reasoning (for example, solving problems, debating, or reflecting on decisions) so those mental processes become stronger. Step 2: Seek feedback and reflect to correct biases and refine techniques — this gradual improvement shows practice is necessary. Options b (intuition) and c (luck) are unreliable foundations for consistent critical thinking, and d (conformity) actually discourages independent analysis, so the correct answer is a: Practice.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
What is one method the text suggests for mitigating risks associated with technology?

Options:
a. Increased regulation
b. Less education
c. Ignoring the risks
d. Outsourcing technology


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Identify the claim in the text — it recommends proactive measures to reduce technology-related harms, and among the options only increased regulation fits that description.  
Step 2: Reasoning — increased regulation creates standards, oversight, and accountability (e.g., safety rules, audits, compliance requirements) that directly mitigate misuse and unintended consequences.  
Step 3: Why other options are wrong — less education would worsen the problem, ignoring the risks does nothing to reduce them, and outsourcing technology may shift but not eliminate risks or accountability.  
Therefore the correct answer is a: Increased regulation.

Explanation:

In research, a __________ is a statement that can be tested and proven true or false.

Options:
a. Hypothesis
b. Theory
c. Conclusion
d. Assumption


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Identify the key phrase "can be tested and proven true or false" — this describes a statement that is empirically testable and falsifiable.  
Step 2: Compare options: a hypothesis is a specific, testable prediction; a theory is a broader explanatory framework built from many tested hypotheses; a conclusion is the outcome drawn after testing; an assumption is a premise taken without test.  
Step 3: Therefore the correct answer is (a) Hypothesis because it is explicitly designed to be tested and shown true or false.

c. Referencing
d. Paraphrasing


Correct Answer: ক

Step 2: Therefore the correct choice is option a: Plagiarism.  
Step 3: Options b (Citation) and c (Referencing) are practices that properly give credit to original authors, and d (Paraphrasing) means rewording someone’s idea (which still requires citation); none of these denote the unethical act itself.

Question #393 (ID: 44969)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A __________ is a systematic investigation to establish facts or principles.

Options:
a. Survey
b. Experiment
c. Case study
d. Review


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
সমাধান:
ধাপে ধাপে বিশ্লেষণ করে দেখা যাক—

ধাপ ১: প্রশ্নের কথ্য সংজ্ঞা অনুযায়ী "systematic investigation to establish facts or principles" হলো এমন একটি নিয়ন্ত্রিত ও পরিকল্পিত তদন্ত যার মাধ্যমে সত্য বা सिद्धান্ত নির্ণয় করা হয় — এটি পরীক্ষার প্রকৃতি।  
ধাপ ২: অপশনগুলোর মানে সংক্ষেপে: ক সার্ভে (তথ্য সংগ্রহ), খ এক্সপেরিমেন্ট (পরীক্ষা), গ কেস স্টাডি (একক ক্ষেত্রে গভীর অধ্যয়ন), ঘ রিভিউ (বিদ্যমান কাজের সারাংশ)।  
ধাপ ৩: কারণ: এক্সপেরিমেন্টই নিয়ন্ত্রিতভাবে পরিবর্তন করে কারণ-প্রভাব পরীক্ষা করে এবং মৌলিক নীতিমালা প্রতিষ্ঠা করতে ব্যবহৃত হয়; অন্যগুলো সাধারণত তথ্য সংগ্রহ, একক বিশ্লেষণ বা পুরনো কাজের সংকলন, যা সরাসরি নিয়ন্ত্রিতভাবে নীতির প্রমাণ স্থাপন করে না।  

অতএব সঠিক উত্তর হলো খ.

Explanation:

Question #422 (ID: 44909)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Quantum physics deals with the behavior of very large objects.

Options:
a. True
b. False


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Define the domain — quantum physics studies the behavior of particles and systems at atomic and subatomic scales (electrons, photons, atoms), i.e., very small objects, not macroscopic ones.  
Step 2: Distinguish from classical physics — macroscopic or very large objects are described accurately by classical mechanics; quantum effects become important when the action [math]S[/math] is comparable to Planck’s constant, e.g., [math]S \sim \hbar[/math].  
Step 3: Conclusion — the statement is false, so the correct answer is b. Option a is incorrect because it reverses the scale at which quantum mechanics is applicable.

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #423 (ID: 44910)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In quantum physics, particles can exist in multiple states __________.

Options:
a. simultaneously
b. sequentially
c. independently
d. exclusively


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
1. Quantum systems obey the superposition principle: a particle's state can be a linear combination of basis states, e.g. [math]|\psi\rangle = c_1|\psi_1\rangle + c_2|\psi_2\rangle[/math], which means the particle effectively occupies multiple possible states at once.
2. Upon measurement the superposition collapses to one outcome, but before measurement the correct description is that the particle exists simultaneously in those component states.
3. Therefore option (a) "simultaneously" is correct; (b) "sequentially" and (c) "independently" are misleading because they imply temporal ordering or separability, and (d) "exclusively" contradicts the superposition principle.

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #424 (ID: 44911)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Name a principle associated with quantum physics.

Options:


Correct Answer: Heisenberg Uncertainty Principle

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Identify the principle that is inherently quantum — the Heisenberg Uncertainty Principle is a fundamental quantum statement about measurement limits.  
Step 2: State the principle and its formula: [math]\Delta x\,\Delta p \ge \frac{\hbar}{2}[/math], which means position and momentum cannot both be known arbitrarily precisely.  
Step 3: Reasoning: this arises from the wave-like nature of particles and the noncommuting operators for position and momentum in quantum mechanics, so the correct answer is Heisenberg Uncertainty Principle.  
Step 4: Other familiar principles like Newton's laws or conservation laws are classical or general and do not express this intrinsic quantum measurement limit, so they are not the best choice.

Explanation:

The other choices (a, c, d) — classical mechanics, thermodynamics, and fluid dynamics — are primarily macroscopic classical theories and not applications that uniquely rely on quantum principles.

Question #426 (ID: 44913)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Quantum entanglement is a phenomenon where particles become correlated.

Options:
a. True
b. False


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
Solution:
Step 1: Quantum entanglement is a quantum-mechanical correlation between two or more particles such that the joint state cannot be written as a product of individual states; their measurement outcomes are linked even when spatially separated.  
Step 2: A simple example is a Bell state [math]\frac{|00\rangle + |11\rangle}{\sqrt{2}}[/math], for which if one particle is measured and found in state [math]|0\rangle[/math], the other is instantly known to be [math]|0\rangle[/math], and similarly for [math]|1\rangle[/math].  
Step 3: Because measurements on one particle determine the correlated outcome of the other (violating separability but not causality), the statement “Quantum entanglement is a phenomenon where particles become correlated” is true.  
Therefore the correct answer is a; option b is incorrect because it denies this well-established quantum phenomenon.

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

================================================================================
Question #427 (ID: 44914)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: পৌরনীতি ও নাগরিকতা | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The principle that states that certain pairs of physical properties cannot be simultaneously known is called __________.

Options:
a. Quantum Superposition
b. Heisenberg Uncertainty
c. Quantum Tunneling
d. Wave Function Collapse


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Solution:
The principle is the Heisenberg Uncertainty Principle, which states that certain pairs of observables (like position and momentum) cannot both be known arbitrarily precisely; their uncertainties satisfy [math]\Delta x\,\Delta p \ge \hbar/2[/math]. Therefore the correct choice is option b, Heisenberg Uncertainty. The other options are different concepts: Quantum Superposition (a) refers to a system being in a combination of states, Quantum Tunneling (c) describes penetration through a potential barrier, and Wave Function Collapse (d) describes the change of the wavefunction upon measurement.

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:
